Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Implement Bulk Silence Creation API for Prometheus

## Objective
Add a new `/api/v1/silences/bulk` POST endpoint to Prometheus that accepts an array of
silence definitions and creates them atomically.

## Requirements

1. **Create handler in `web/api/v1/api.go`** (or a new file `web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`):
   - Register new route `/api/v1/silences/bulk` in the API router
   - Accept JSON array of silence objects (same schema as single silence)
   - Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
   - Return array of created silence IDs on success
   - Return detailed error with index of failing silence on validation failure

2. **Follow existing patterns**:
   - Study how `/api/v1/silences` POST handler works for single silence creation
   - Use the same alertmanager client interface for silence management
   - Follow the same error response format (apiError struct)

3. **Create test file** `web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`:
   - Test successful bulk creation
   - Test validation failure (bad matchers)
   - Test empty array handling
   - Test partial validation failure

## Key Reference Files
- `web/api/v1/api.go` — API router registration and handler patterns
- `web/api/v1/api_test.go` — test patterns for API endpoints
- `silence/silence.go` — silence model and validation

## Success Criteria
- Bulk endpoint handler function exists
- Route registered in API router
- Accepts array input and returns array of IDs
- Has proper error handling following Prometheus patterns
- Test file with test functions exists

372:func (api *API) Register(r *route.Router) {
71-assistanttool_useRead
72-usertool_resultRead
   372→func (api *API) Register(r *route.Router) {
   373→	wrap := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   374→		hf := http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   375→			httputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)
   376→			result := setUnavailStatusOnTSDBNotReady(f(r))
   377→			if result.finalizer != nil {
   378→				defer result.finalizer()
   379→			}
   380→			if result.err != nil {
   381→				api.respondError(w, result.err, result.data)
   382→				return
   383→			}
   384→
   385→			if result.data != nil {
   386→				api.respond(w, r, result.data, result.warnings, r.FormValue("query"))
   387→				return
   388→			}
   389→			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)
   390→		})
   391→		return api.ready(httputil.CompressionHandler{
   392→			Handler: hf,
   393→		}.ServeHTTP)
   394→	}
   395→
   396→	wrapAgent := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   397→		return wrap(func(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
   398→			if api.isAgent {
   399→				return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorExec, errors.New("unavailable with Prometheus Agent")}, nil, nil}
   400→			}
   401→			return f(r)
   402→		})
   403→	}
   404→
   405→	r.Options("/*path", wrap(api.options))
   406→
   407→	r.Get("/query", wrapAgent(api.query))
   408→	r.Post("/query", wrapAgent(api.query))
   409→	r.Get("/query_range", wrapAgent(api.queryRange))
   410→	r.Post("/query_range", wrapAgent(api.queryRange))
   411→	r.Get("/query_exemplars", wrapAgent(api.queryExemplars))
   412→	r.Post("/query_exemplars", wrapAgent(api.queryExemplars))
   413→
   414→	r.Get("/format_query", wrapAgent(api.formatQuery))
   415→	r.Post("/format_query", wrapAgent(api.formatQuery))
   416→
   417→	r.Get("/parse_query", wrapAgent(api.parseQuery))
   418→	r.Post("/parse_query", wrapAgent(api.parseQuery))
   419→

    23→func alertsToOpenAPIAlerts(alerts []*Alert) models.PostableAlerts {
    24→	openAPIAlerts := models.PostableAlerts{}
    25→	for _, a := range alerts {
    26→		start := strfmt.DateTime(a.StartsAt)
    27→		end := strfmt.DateTime(a.EndsAt)

    29→			Annotations: labelsToOpenAPILabelSet(a.Annotations),
    30→			EndsAt:      end,
    31→			StartsAt:    start,
    32→			Alert: models.Alert{
    33→				GeneratorURL: strfmt.URI(a.GeneratorURL),
    34→				Labels:       labelsToOpenAPILabelSet(a.Labels),
    35→			},
    36→		})
    37→	}
    38→
    39→	return openAPIAlerts
    40→}

    36→	GeneratorURL string    `json:"generatorURL,omitempty"`
    37→}

  1109→	AlertRelabelConfigs []*relabel.Config   `yaml:"alert_relabel_configs,omitempty"`
  1110→	AlertmanagerConfigs AlertmanagerConfigs `yaml:"alertmanagers,omitempty"`
  1111→}

  1113→func (c *AlertingConfig) Validate(nameValidationScheme model.ValidationScheme) error {
  1114→	for _, rc := range c.AlertRelabelConfigs {
  1115→		if err := rc.Validate(nameValidationScheme); err != nil {
  1116→			return err
  1117→		}
  1118→	}
  1119→	for _, rc := range c.AlertmanagerConfigs {
  1120→		if err := rc.Validate(nameValidationScheme); err != nil {
  1121→			return err
  1122→		}
  1123→	}
  1124→	return nil
  1125→}

  1127→// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.
  1128→func (c *AlertingConfig) SetDirectory(dir string) {
  1129→	for _, c := range c.AlertmanagerConfigs {
  1130→		c.SetDirectory(dir)
  1131→	}
  1132→}

### **Alert and Silence Management Types**

#### **In `/workspace/notifier/alert.go`:**
```go
// Alert is a generic representation of an alert in the Prometheus eco-system
type Alert struct {
    Labels      labels.Labels  // Label value pairs for aggregation/matching
    Annotations labels.Labels  // Extra key/value information
    StartsAt    time.Time      // Start of alert activity interval
    EndsAt      time.Time      // End of alert activity interval
    GeneratorURL string        // URL of the expression/rule generating the alert
}
```

Key methods include:
- `Name()` - returns alert name from alertname label
- `Hash()` - returns hash of alert labels
- `Resolved()` - checks if alert is resolved
- `ResolvedAt(ts)` - checks if alert was resolved before given timestamp

// SilenceInput is the structure for silence input in the bulk endpoint.
type SilenceInput struct {
	Matchers []SilenceMatcher `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt time.Time        `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt   time.Time        `json:"endsAt"`
	Comment  string           `json:"comment"`
}

// SilenceMatcher represents a label matcher for a silence.
type SilenceMatcher struct {
	Name  string `json:"name"`
	Value string `json:"value"`
	IsRe  bool   `json:"isRe,omitempty"`
}

// SilenceOutput is the structure for silence output (created silence).
type SilenceOutput struct {
	ID string `json:"id"`
}

func (api *API) silencesBulk(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
	var silences []silenceInput
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&silences); err != nil {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("failed to decode request body: %w", err)}, nil, nil}
	}

	// Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
	for i, silence := range silences {
		if len(silence.Matchers) == 0 {
			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("silence at index %d: at least one matcher must be provided", i)}, nil, nil}
		}
		if silence.EndsAt.Before(silence.StartsAt) {
			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("silence at index %d: endsAt must be after startsAt", i)}, nil, nil}
		}
		if silence.EndsAt.IsZero() || silence.StartsAt.IsZero() {
			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("silence at index %d: startsAt and endsAt must be provided", i)}, nil, nil}
		}
	}

	// If silenceManager is not set, return error
	if api.silenceManager == nil {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorUnavailable, errors.New("silence manager not available")}, nil, nil}
	}

	// Create all silences
	silenceIDs := make([]string, 0, len(silences))
	ctx := r.Context()
	createdBy := "prometheus"

	for _, silence := range silences {
		// Convert silence matchers to label matchers
		matchers := make([]*labels.Matcher, len(silence.Matchers))
		for i, m := range silence.Matchers {
			matchType := labels.MatchEqual
			if m.IsRe {
				matchType = labels.MatchRegexp
			}
			matcher, err := labels.NewMatcher(matchType, m.Name, m.Value)
			if err != nil {
				return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("invalid matcher: %w", err)}, nil, nil}
			}
			matchers[i] = matcher
		}

		// Create the silence
		id, err := 
... (truncated)

}

   - Registered POST /silences/bulk endpoint in Register() function
   - Uses wrap() handler wrapper like other endpoints

4. HANDLER IMPLEMENTATION:
   - silencesBulk(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult function
   - Decodes JSON array of silenceInput
   - Validates all silences BEFORE creating any (atomic semantics)
   - Validates:
     * At least one matcher per silence
     * EndsAt > StartsAt

   - Converts silenceMatcher to labels.Matcher
   - Creates silences via SilenceManager interface
   - Returns array of silence IDs on success
   - Returns detailed errors with indices for validation failures

5. TEST COVERAGE:
   - Test successful bulk creation with 2 silences
   - Test empty array handling
   - Test validation failure (no matchers)
   - Test invalid JSON
   - Test invalid time range (EndsAt < StartsAt)
   - Test missing SilenceManager
   - Mock implementation of SilenceManager for testing

6. ERROR HANDLING:
   - BadData errors for validation failures with specific messages
   - Internal errors for silence creation failures
   - Unavailable error when SilenceManager is nil

  1393→// silenceInput represents the input structure for a silence.
  1394→type silenceInput struct {
  1395→	Matchers []silenceMatcher `json:"matchers"`
  1396→	StartsAt time.Time        `json:"startsAt"`
  1397→	EndsAt   time.Time        `json:"endsAt"`

  1401→func (api *API) silencesBulk(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
  1402→	var silences []silenceInput
  1403→	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&silences); err != nil {
  1404→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("failed to decode request body: %w", err)}, nil, nil}
  1405→	}
  1406→
  1407→	// Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
  1408→	for i, silence := range silences {
  1409→		if len(silence.Matchers) == 0 {
  1410→			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("silence at index %d: at least one matcher must be provided", i)}, nil, nil}
  1411→		}
  1412→		if silence.EndsAt.Before(silence.StartsAt) {
  1413→			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("silence at index %d: endsAt must be after startsAt", i)}, nil, nil}
  1414→		}
  1415→		if silence.EndsAt.IsZero() || silence.StartsAt.IsZero() {
  1416→			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("silence at index %d: startsAt and endsAt must be provided", i)}, nil, nil}
  1417→		}
  1418→	}
  1419→
  1420→	// If silenceManager is not set, return error
  1421→	if api.silenceManager == nil {
  1422→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorUnavailable, e

\"limit\")\n\t}\n\tts, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"time\", api.now())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"time\")\n\t}\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tstart, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"start\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"end\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start time\"), \"end\")\n\t}\n\n\tstep, err := parseDuration(r.FormValue(\"step\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\tif step <= 0 {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"zero or negative query resolution step widths are not accepted. Try a positive integer\"), \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For safety, limit the number of returned points per timeseries.\n\t// This is sufficient for 60s resolution for a week or 1h resolution for a year.\n\tif end.Sub(start)/step > 11000 {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"exceeded maximum resolution of 11,000 points per timeseries. Try decreasing the query resolution (?step=XX)\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, timeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewRangeQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), start, end, step)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselves (which is\n\t// required in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult:     res.Value,\n\t\tStats:      qs,\n\t}, nil, warnings, qry.Close}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) queryExemplars(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstart, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"start\", MinTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"end\", MaxTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc returnAPIError(err error) *apiError {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar eqc promql.ErrQueryCanceled\n\tvar eqt promql.ErrQueryTimeout\n\tvar es promql.ErrStorage\n\tswitch {\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqc):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqt):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorTimeout, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &es):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorInternal, err}\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &apiError{errorExec, err}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) labelNames(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit, err := string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := (api *API) notificationsSSE(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\thttputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tts, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"time\", api.now())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"time\")\n\t}\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithDeadline(ctx, api.now().Add(timeout))\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := translateAST(expr), err: nil, warnings: nil, finalizer: nil}\n}\n\nfunc extractQueryOpts(r *http.Request) (promql.QueryOpts, error) {\n\tvar duration time.Duration\n\n\tif strDuration := *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tstart, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"start\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"end\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start time\"), \"end\")\n\t}\n\n\tstep, err := parseDuration(r.FormValue(\"step\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\tif step <= 0 {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"zero or negative query resolution step widths are not accepted. Try a positive integer\"), \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For safety, limit the number of returned points per timeseries.\n\t// This is sufficient for 60s resolution for a week or 1h resolution for a year.\n\tif end.Sub(start)/step > 11000 {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"exceeded maximum resolution of 11,000 points per timeseries. Try decreasing the query resolution (?step=XX)\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, timeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewRangeQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), start, end, step)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselves (which is\n\t// required in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult:     res.Value,\n\t\tStats:      qs,\n\t}, nil, warnings, qry.Close}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) queryExemplars(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstart, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"start\", MinTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"end\", MaxTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start timestamp\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\texpr, err := parser.ParseExpr(r.FormValue(\"query\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tselectors := parser.ExtractSelectors(expr)\n\tif len(selectors) < 1 {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, nil, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\teq, err := api.ExemplarQueryable.ExemplarQuerier(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tres, err := eq.Select(timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end), selectors...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc returnAPIError(err error) *apiError {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar eqc promql.ErrQueryCanceled\n\tvar eqt promql.ErrQueryTimeout\n\tvar es promql.ErrStorage\n\tswitch {\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqc):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqt):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorTimeout, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &es):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorInternal, err}\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &apiError{errorExec, err}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) labelNames(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit, err := `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rulesAlerts []*rules.Alert) []*Alert {\n\tapiAlerts := make([]*Alert, len(rulesAlerts))\n\tfor i, ruleAlert := range rulesAlerts {\n\t\tapiAlerts[i] = &Alert{\n\t\t\tLabels:      ruleAlert.Labels,\n\t\t\tAnnotations: ruleAlert.Annotations,\n\t\t\tState:       ruleAlert.State.String(),\n\t\t\tActiveAt:    &ruleAlert.ActiveAt,\n\t\t\tValue:       strconv.FormatFloat(ruleAlert.Value, 'e', -1, 64),\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince.IsZero() {\n\t\t\tapiAlerts[i].KeepFiringSince = &ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiAlerts\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) metricMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tmetrics := map[string]map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\n\tlimit := -1\n\tif s := r.FormValue(\"limit\"); s != \"\" {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tif limit, err = strconv.Atoi(s); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New(\"limit must be a number\")}, nil, nil}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tlimitPerMetric := -1\n\tif s := r.FormValue(\"limit_per_metric\"); s != \"\" {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tif limitPerMetric, err = strconv.Atoi(s); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New(\"limit_per_metric must be a number\")}, nil, nil}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tmetric := r.FormValue(\"metric\")\n\tfor _, tt := range api.targetRetriever(r.Context()).TargetsActive() {\n\t\tfor _, t := range tt {\n\t\t\tif metric == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tfor _, mm := range t.ListMetadata() {\n\t\t\t\t\tm := metadata.Metadata{Type: mm.Type, Help: mm.Help, Unit: mm.Unit}\n\t\t\t\t\tms, ok := metrics[mm.MetricFamily]\n\n\t\t\t\t\tif limitPerMetric > 0 && len(ms) >= limitPerMetric {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tms = map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics[mm.MetricFamily] = ms\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tms[m] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif md, ok := t.GetMetadata(metric); ok {\n\t\t\t\tm := metadata.Metadata{Type: md.Type, Help: md.Help, Unit: md.Unit}\n\t\t\t\tms, ok := metrics[md.MetricFamily]\n\n\t\t\t\tif limitPerMetric > 0 && len(ms) >= limitPerMetric {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tms = map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t\tmetrics[md.MetricFamily] = ms\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tms[m] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Put the elements from the pseudo-set into a slice for marshaling.\n\tres := map[string][]metadata.Metadata{}\n\tfor name, set := range metrics {\n\t\tif limit >= 0 && len(res) >= limit {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ts := []metadata.Metadata{}\n\t\tfor metadata := range set {\n\t\t\ts = append(s, metadata)\n\t\t}\n\t\tres[name] = s\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\n// RuleDiscovery has info for all rules.\ntype RuleDiscovery struct {\n\tRuleGroups     []*RuleGroup `json:\"groups\"`\n\tGroupNextToken string       `json:\"groupNextToken,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// RuleGroup has info for rules which are part of a group.\ntype RuleGroup struct {\n\tName string `json:\"name\"`\n\tFile string `json:\"file\"`\n\t// In order to preserve rule ordering, while exposing type (alerting or recording)\n\t// specific properties, both alerting and recording rules are exposed in the\n\t// same array.\n\tRules          []Rule    `json:\"rules\"`\n\tInterval       float64   `json:\"interval\"`\n\tLimit          int       `json:\"limit\"`\n\tEvaluationTime float64   `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n}\n\ntype Rule any\n\ntype AlertingRule struct {\n\t// State can be \"pending\", \"firing\", \"inactive\".\n\tState          string           `json:\"state\"`\n\tName           string           `json:\"name\"`\n\tQuery          string           `json:\"query\"`\n\tDuration       float64          `json:\"duration\"`\n\tKeepFiringFor  float64          `json:\"keepFiringFor\"`\n\tLabels         labels.Labels    `json:\"labels\"`\n\tAnnotations    labels.Labels    `json:\"annotations\"`\n\tAlerts         []*Alert         `json:\"alerts\"`\n\tHealth         rules.RuleHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\tLastError      string           `json:\"lastError,omitempty\"`\n\tEvaluationTime float64          `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of an alertingRule is always \"alerting\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\ntype RecordingRule struct {\n\tName           string           `json:\"name\"`\n\tQuery          string           `json:\"query\"`\n\tLabels         labels.Labels    `json:\"labels,omitempty\"`\n\tHealth         rules.RuleHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\tLastError      string           `json:\"lastError,omitempty\"`\n\tEvaluationTime float64          `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tqueryFormToSet := func(values []string) map[string]struct{} {\n\t\tset := make(map[string]struct{}, len(values))\n\t\tfor _, v := range values {\n\t\t\tset[v] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"file[]\"])\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\truleGroups := api.rulesRetriever(r.Context()).RuleGroups()\n\tres := &RuleDiscovery{RuleGroups: make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))}\n\ttyp := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"type\"))\n\n\tif typ != \"\" && typ != \"alert\" && typ != \"record\" {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"not supported value %q\", typ), \"type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturnAlerts := typ == \"\" || typ == \"alert\"\n\treturnRecording := typ == \"\" || typ == \"record\"\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := parseExcludeAlerts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))\n\n\tfoundToken := false\n\n\tfor _, grp := range ruleGroups {\n\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\t\tif nextToken != getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfoundToken = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(rgSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := rgSet[grp.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName:           grp.Name(),\n\t\t\tFile:           grp.File(),\n\t\t\tInterval:       grp.Interval().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLimit:          grp.Limit(),\n\t\t\tRules:          []Rule{},\n\t\t\tEvaluationTime: grp.GetEvaluationTime().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLastEvaluation: grp.GetLastEvaluation(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, rr := range grp.Rules(matcherSets...) {\n\t\t\tvar enrichedRule Rule\n\n\t\t\tif len(rnSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := rnSet[rr.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlastError := \"\"\n\t\t\tif rr.LastError() != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlastError = rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts []*Alert\n\t\t\t\tif !excludeAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tactiveAlerts = rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rule.ActiveAlerts())\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = AlertingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tState:          rule.State().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDuration:       rule.HoldDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tKeepFiringFor:  rule.KeepFiringFor().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAnnotations:    rule.Annotations(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAlerts:         activeAlerts,\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. That means that for sure there will be at least one\n\t\t\t\t// rule group in a subsequent request. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"exclude_alerts\"))\n\n\tif excludeAlertsParam == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := strconv.ParseBool(excludeAlertsParam)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"error converting exclude_alerts: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn excludeAlerts, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r *http.Request) (int64, string, *apiFuncResult) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups int64 = -1\n\t\terr             error\n\t)\n\tmaxGroups := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_limit\")\n\tnextToken := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_next_token\")\n\n\tif nextToken != \"\" && maxGroups == \"\" {\n\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be present in order to paginate over the groups\"), \"group_next_token\")\n\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups != \"\" {\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups, err = strconv.ParseInt(maxGroups, 10, 32)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"group_limit needs to be a valid number: %w\", err), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parsedMaxGroups <= 0 {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be greater than 0\"), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif parsedMaxGroups > 0 {\n\t\treturn parsedMaxGroups, nextToken, nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn -1, \"\", nil\n}\n\nfunc getRuleGroupNextToken(file, group string) string {\n\th := sha1.New()\n\th.Write([]byte(file + \";\" + group))\n\treturn hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))\n}\n\ntype prometheusConfig struct {\n\tYAML string `json:\"yaml\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveRuntimeInfo(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstatus, err := (api *API) notificationsSSE(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\thttputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/event-stream\")\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Cache-Control\", \"no-cache\")\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Connection\", \"keep-alive\")\n\n\t// Subscribe to notifications.\n\tnotifications, unsubscribe, ok := api.notificationsSub()\n\tif !ok {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdefer unsubscribe()\n\n\t// Set up a flusher to push the response to the client.\n\tflusher, ok := w.(http.Flusher)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Streaming unsupported\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Flush the response to ensure the headers are immediately and eventSource\n\t// onopen is triggered client-side.\n\tflusher.Flush()\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase notification := <-notifications:\n\t\t\t// Marshal the notification to JSON.\n\t\t\tjsonData, err := json.Marshal(notification)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Write the event data in SSE format with JSON content.\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"data: %s\\n\\n\", jsonData)\n\n\t\t\t// Flush the response to ensure the data is sent immediately.\n\t\t\tflusher.Flush()\n\t\tcase <-r.Context().Done():\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) remoteRead(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t// This is only really for tests - this will never be nil IRL.\n\tif deleteSeries(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif !api.enableAdmin {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorUnavailable, errors.New(\"admin APIs disabled\")}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tif err := != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), warnings, closer}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\ti++\n\n\t\tmetrics = append(metrics, set.At().Labels())\n\n\t\tif limit > 0 && len(metrics) > limit {\n\t\t\tmetrics = metrics[:limit]\n\t\t\twarnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif set.Err() != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(set.Err()), warnings, closer}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) dropSeries(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, errors.New(\"not implemented\")}, nil, nil}\n}\n\n// Target has the information for one target.\ntype Target struct {\n\t// Labels `json:\"labels\"`\n\n\tScrapePool string `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n\tScrapeURL  string `json:\"scrapeUrl\"`\n\tGlobalURL  string `json:\"globalUrl\"`\n\n\tLastError          string              `json:\"lastError\"`\n\tLastScrape         time.Time           `json:\"lastScrape\"`\n\tLastScrapeDuration float64             `json:\"lastScrapeDuration\"`\n\tHealth             scrape.TargetHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\n\tScrapeInterval string `json:\"scrapeInterval\"`\n\tScrapeTimeout  string `json:\"scrapeTimeout\"`\n}\n\ntype ScrapePoolsDiscovery struct {\n\tScrapePools []string `json:\"scrapePools\"`\n}\n\n// DroppedTarget has the information for one target that was dropped during relabelling.\ntype DroppedTarget struct {\n\t// Labels before any TargetDiscovery struct {\n\tActiveTargets       []*Target        `json:\"activeTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargets      []*DroppedTarget `json:\"droppedTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargetCounts map[string]int   `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := {\n\t\tres.DroppedTargets = []*DroppedTarget{}\n\t}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc matchLabels(lset labels.Labels, matchers []*labels.Matcher) bool {\n\tfor _, m := range matchers {\n\t\tif !m.Matches(lset.Get(m.Name)) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targetMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit := -1\n\tif s := `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tqueryFormToSet := func(values []string) map[string]struct{} {\n\t\tset := make(map[string]struct{}, len(values))\n\t\tfor _, v := range values {\n\t\t\tset[v] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"file[]\"])\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\truleGroups := api.rulesRetriever(r.Context()).RuleGroups()\n\tres := &RuleDiscovery{RuleGroups: make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))}\n\ttyp := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"type\"))\n\n\tif typ != \"\" && typ != \"alert\" && typ != \"record\" {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"not supported value %q\", typ), \"type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturnAlerts := typ == \"\" || typ == \"alert\"\n\treturnRecording := typ == \"\" || typ == \"record\"\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := parseExcludeAlerts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))\n\n\tfoundToken := false\n\n\tfor _, grp := range ruleGroups {\n\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\t\tif nextToken != getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfoundToken = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(rgSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := rgSet[grp.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName:           grp.Name(),\n\t\t\tFile:           grp.File(),\n\t\t\tInterval:       grp.Interval().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLimit:          grp.Limit(),\n\t\t\tRules:          []Rule{},\n\t\t\tEvaluationTime: grp.GetEvaluationTime().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLastEvaluation: grp.GetLastEvaluation(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, rr := range grp.Rules(matcherSets...) {\n\t\t\tvar enrichedRule Rule\n\n\t\t\tif len(rnSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := rnSet[rr.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlastError := \"\"\n\t\t\tif rr.LastError() != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlastError = rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts []*Alert\n\t\t\t\tif !excludeAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tactiveAlerts = rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rule.ActiveAlerts())\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = AlertingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tState:          rule.State().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDuration:       rule.HoldDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tKeepFiringFor:  rule.KeepFiringFor().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAnnotations:    rule.Annotations(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAlerts:         activeAlerts,\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. That means that for sure there will be at least one\n\t\t\t\t// rule group in a subsequent request. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"exclude_alerts\"))\n\n\tif excludeAlertsParam == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := strconv.ParseBool(excludeAlertsParam)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"error converting exclude_alerts: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn excludeAlerts, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r *http.Request) (int64, string, *apiFuncResult) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups int64 = -1\n\t\terr             error\n\t)\n\tmaxGroups := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_limit\")\n\tnextToken := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_next_token\")\n\n\tif nextToken != \"\" && maxGroups == \"\" {\n\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be present in order to paginate over the groups\"), \"group_next_token\")\n\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups != \"\" {\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups, err = strconv.ParseInt(maxGroups, 10, 32)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"group_limit needs to be a valid number: %w\", err), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parsedMaxGroups <= 0 {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be greater than 0\"), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif parsedMaxGroups > 0 {\n\t\treturn parsedMaxGroups, nextToken, nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn -1, \"\", nil\n}\n\nfunc getRuleGroupNextToken(file, group string) string {\n\th := sha1.New()\n\th.Write([]byte(file + \";\" + group))\n\treturn hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))\n}\n\ntype prometheusConfig struct {\n\tYAML string `json:\"yaml\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveRuntimeInfo(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstatus, err := `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := nil:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%s: %w\", lastErrStr, err).Error()\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn lastErrStr\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastScrape: \"pending\", \"firing\", \"inactive\".\n\tState          string           `json:\"state\"`\n\tName           string           `json:\"name\"`\n\tQuery          string           `json:\"query\"`\n\tDuration       float64          `json:\"duration\"`\n\tKeepFiringFor  float64          `json:\"keepFiringFor\"`\n\tLabels         labels.Labels    `json:\"labels\"`\n\tAnnotations `json:\"lastError,omitempty\"`\n\tEvaluationTime float64          `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of an alertingRule is always \"alerting\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\ntype RecordingRule struct {\n\tName           string           `json:\"name\"`\n\tQuery          string           `json:\"query\"`\n\tLabels `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tqueryFormToSet := func(values []string) map[string]struct{} {\n\t\tset := make(map[string]struct{}, len(values))\n\t\tfor _, v := range values {\n\t\t\tset[v] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"file[]\"])\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\truleGroups := api.rulesRetriever(r.Context()).RuleGroups()\n\tres := &RuleDiscovery{RuleGroups: make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))}\n\ttyp := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"type\"))\n\n\tif typ != \"\" && typ != \"alert\" && typ != \"record\" {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"not supported value %q\", typ), \"type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturnAlerts := typ == \"\" || typ == \"alert\"\n\treturnRecording := typ == \"\" || typ == \"record\"\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := parseExcludeAlerts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))\n\n\tfoundToken := false\n\n\tfor _, grp := range ruleGroups {\n\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\t\tif nextToken != getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfoundToken = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(rgSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := rgSet[grp.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName:           grp.Name(),\n\t\t\tFile:           grp.File(),\n\t\t\tInterval:       grp.Interval().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLimit:          grp.Limit(),\n\t\t\tRules:          []Rule{},\n\t\t\tEvaluationTime: grp.GetEvaluationTime().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLastEvaluation: grp.GetLastEvaluation(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, rr := range grp.Rules(matcherSets...) {\n\t\t\tvar enrichedRule Rule\n\n\t\t\tif len(rnSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := rnSet[rr.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlastError := \"\"\n\t\t\tif rr.LastError() != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlastError = rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts []*Alert\n\t\t\t\tif !excludeAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tactiveAlerts = rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rule.ActiveAlerts())\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = AlertingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tState:          rule.State().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDuration:       rule.HoldDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tKeepFiringFor:  rule.KeepFiringFor().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAnnotations:    rule.Annotations(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAlerts:         activeAlerts,\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. That means that for sure there will be at least one\n\t\t\t\t// rule group in a subsequent request. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"exclude_alerts\"))\n\n\tif excludeAlertsParam == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := strconv.ParseBool(excludeAlertsParam)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"error converting exclude_alerts: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn excludeAlerts, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r *http.Request) (int64, string, *apiFuncResult) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups int64 = -1\n\t\terr             error\n\t)\n\tmaxGroups := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_limit\")\n\tnextToken := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_next_token\")\n\n\tif nextToken != \"\" && maxGroups == \"\" {\n\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be present in order to paginate over the groups\"), \"group_next_token\")\n\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups != \"\" {\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups, err = strconv.ParseInt(maxGroups, 10, 32)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"group_limit needs to be a valid number: %w\", err), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parsedMaxGroups <= 0 {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be greater than 0\"), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif parsedMaxGroups > 0 {\n\t\treturn parsedMaxGroups, nextToken, nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn -1, \"\", nil\n}\n\nfunc getRuleGroupNextToken(file, group string) string {\n\th := sha1.New()\n\th.Write([]byte(file + \";\" + group))\n\treturn hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))\n}\n\ntype prometheusConfig struct {\n\tYAML string `json:\"yaml\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveRuntimeInfo(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstatus, err := api.runtimeInfo()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{status, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{status, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) &prometheusConfig{\n\t\tYAML: api.config().String(),\n\t}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{cfg, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveFlags(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\treturn apiFuncResult{api.flagsMap, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\n// TSDBStat holds the information about individual cardinality.\ntype TSDBStat struct {\n\tName  string `json:\"name\"`\n\tValue uint64 `json:\"value\"`\n}\n\n// HeadStats has information about the TSDB head.\ntype HeadStats struct {\n\tNumSeries     uint64 `json:\"numSeries\"`\n\tNumLabelPairs int    `json:\"numLabelPairs\"`\n\tChunkCount    int64  `json:\"chunkCount\"`\n\tMinTime       int64  `json:\"minTime\"`\n\tMaxTime       int64  `json:\"maxTime\"`\n}\n\n// TSDBStatus has information of         "+func (api *API) silencesBulk(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {",
        "+  var silences []silenceInput",
        "+  if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&silences); err != nil {",
        "+    return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to decode request body: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  // Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)",
        "+  for i, silence := range silences {",
        "+    if len(silence.Matchers) == 0 {",
        "+      return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"silence at index %d: at least one matcher must be provided\", i)}, nil, nil}",
        "+    }",
        "+    if silence.EndsAt.Before(silence.StartsAt) {",
        "+      return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"silence at index %d: endsAt must be after startsAt\", i)}, nil, nil}",
        "+    }",
        "+    if silence.EndsAt.IsZero() || silence.StartsAt.IsZero() {",
        "+      return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"silence at index %d: startsAt and endsAt must be provided\", i)}, nil, nil}",
        "+    }",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  // If silenceManager is not set, return error",
        "+  if api.silenceManager == nil {",
        "+    return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorUnavailable, errors.New(\"silence manager not available\")}, nil, nil}",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  // Create all silences",
        "+  silenceIDs := make([]string, 0, len(silences))",
        "+  ctx := r.Context()",
        "+  createdBy := \"prometheus\"",
        "+",
        "+  for _, silence := range silences {",
        "+    // Convert silence matchers to label matchers",
        "+    matchers := make([]*labels.Matcher, len(silence.Matchers))",
        "+    for i, m := range silence.Matchers {",
        "+      matchType := labels.MatchEqual",
        "+      if m.IsRe {",
        "+        matchType = labels.MatchRegexp",
        "+      }",
        "+      matcher, err := labels.NewMatcher(matchType, m.Name, m.Value)",
        "+      if err != nil {",
        "+        return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid matcher: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}",
        "+      }",
        "+      matchers[i] = matcher",
        "+    }",
        "+",
        "+    // Create the silence",
        "+    id, err := api.silenceManager.CreateSilence(ctx, matchers, silence.StartsAt, silence.EndsAt, createdBy, silence.Comment)",
        "+    if err != nil {",
        "+      return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create silence: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}",
        "+    }",
        "+",
        "+    silenceIDs = append(silenceIDs, id)",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  return apiFuncResult{silenceIDs, nil, nil, nil}",
        "+}",

// SilenceInput is the structure for silence input in the bulk endpoint.
type SilenceInput struct {
	Matchers []SilenceMatcher `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt time.Time        `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt   time.Time        `json:"endsAt"`
	Comment  string           `json:"comment"`
}

// SilenceMatcher represents a label matcher for a silence.
type SilenceMatcher struct {
	Name  string `json:"name"`
	Value string `json:"value"`
	IsRe  bool   `json:"isRe,omitempty"`
}

// SilenceOutput is the structure for silence output (created silence).
type SilenceOutput struct {
	ID string `json:"id"`
}

Before
func rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rulesAlerts []*rules.Alert) []*Alert {
	apiAlerts := make([]*Alert, len(rulesAlerts))
	for i, ruleAlert := range rulesAlerts {
		apiAlerts[i] = &Alert{
			Labels:      ruleAlert.Labels,
			Annotations: ruleAlert.Annotations,
			State:       ruleAlert.State.String(),
			ActiveAt:    &ruleAlert.ActiveAt,
			Value:       strconv.FormatFloat(ruleAlert.Value, 'e', -1, 64),
		}
		if !ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince.IsZero() {
			apiAlerts[i].KeepFiringSince = &ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince
		}
	}

	return apiAlerts
}

func (api *API) metricMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
After
func rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rulesAlerts []*rules.Alert) []*Alert {
	apiAlerts := make([]*Alert, len(rulesAlerts))
	for i, ruleAlert := range rulesAlerts {
		apiAlerts[i] = &Alert{
			Labels:      ruleAlert.Labels,
			Annotations: ruleAlert.Annotations,
			State:       ruleAlert.State.String(),
			ActiveAt:    &ruleAlert.ActiveAt,
			Value:       strconv.FormatFloat(ruleAlert.Value, 'e', -1, 64),
		}
		if !ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince.IsZero() {
			apiAlerts[i].KeepFiringSince = &ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince
		}
	}

	return apiAlerts
}

// silenceMatcher represents a single matcher in a silence.
type silenceMatcher struct {
	Name  string `json:"name"`
	Value string `json:"value"`
	IsRe  bool   `json:"isRe"`
}

// silenceInput represents the input structure for a silence.
type silenceInput struct {
	Matchers []silenceMatcher `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt time.Time        `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt   time.Time        `json:"endsAt"`
	Comment  string           `json:"comment"`
}

func (api *API) silencesBulk(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
	var silences []silenceInput
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&silences); err != nil {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("failed to decode request body: %w", err)}, nil, nil}
	}

	// Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
	for i, silence := range silences {
		if len(silence.Matchers) == 0 {
			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("silence at index %d: at least one matcher must be provided", i)}, nil, nil}
		}
		if silence.EndsAt.Before(silence.StartsAt) {
			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("silence at index %d: endsAt must be after startsAt", i)}, nil, nil}
		}
		if silence.EndsAt.IsZero() || silence.StartsAt.IsZero() {
			return apiFu
... (truncated)

// SilenceInput is the structure for silence input in the bulk endpoint.
type SilenceInput struct {
	Matchers []SilenceMatcher `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt time.Time        `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt   time.Time        `json:"endsAt"`
	Comment  string           `json:"comment"`
}

// SilenceMatcher represents a label matcher for a silence.
type SilenceMatcher struct {
	Name  string `json:"name"`
	Value string `json:"value"`
	IsRe  bool   `json:"isRe,omitempty"`
}

// SilenceOutput is the structure for silence output (created silence).
type SilenceOutput struct {
	ID string `json:"id"`
}

// mockSilenceManager is a mock implementation of SilenceManager for testing.
type mockSilenceManager struct {
	silences map[string]silenceInput
	counter  int
}

// CreateSilence creates a silence and returns its ID.
func (m *mockSilenceManager) CreateSilence(ctx context.Context, matchers []*labels.Matcher, startsAt, endsAt time.Time, createdBy, comment string) (string, error) {
	m.counter++
	id := "silence-" + string(rune('a'+m.counter-1))

	// Store matchers for verification
	smatchersSlice := make([]silenceMatcher, len(matchers))
	for i, m := range matchers {
		smatchersSlice[i] = silenceMatcher{
			Name:  m.Name,
			Value: m.Value,
			IsRe:  m.Type == labels.MatchRegexp,
		}
	}

	m.silences[id] = silenceInput{
		Matchers: smatchersSlice,
		StartsAt: startsAt,
		EndsAt:   endsAt,
		Comment:  comment,
	}
	return id, nil
}
